\ChapterHeader{3}{Chapter 3}

\MainTextVerseMark{3}{1}Καὶ εἰσῆλθεν\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} πάλιν ⸀εἰς συναγωγήν, καὶ ἦν\FnParse{b}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular} ἐκεῖ ἄνθρωπος ἐξηραμμένην\FnParseFormGloss{c}{perfect passive participle accusative feminine singular}{ξηραίνω}{to wither} ἔχων\FnParse{d}{present active participle nominative masculine singular} τὴν χεῖρα. 
\MainTextVerseMark{3}{2}καὶ παρετήρουν\FnParseFormGloss{a}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural}{παρατηρέω}{to watch closely} αὐτὸν εἰ τοῖς σάββασιν θεραπεύσει\FnParse{b}{future active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτόν, ἵνα ⸀κατηγορήσωσιν\FnParseFormGloss{c}{aorist active subjunctive 3rd plural}{κατηγορέω}{to accuse} αὐτοῦ. 
\MainTextVerseMark{3}{3}καὶ λέγει\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 3rd singular} τῷ ἀνθρώπῳ τῷ ⸂τὴν χεῖρα ἔχοντι\FnParse{b}{present active participle dative masculine singular} ξηράν⸃·\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative feminine singular}{ξηρός}{dried up} ⸀Ἔγειρε\FnParse{d}{present active imperative 2nd singular} εἰς τὸ μέσον. 
\MainTextVerseMark{3}{4}καὶ λέγει\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτοῖς· Ἔξεστιν\FnParse{b}{present active indicative 3rd singular} τοῖς σάββασιν ⸀ἀγαθοποιῆσαι\FnParseFormGloss{c}{aorist active infinitive}{ἀγαθοποιέω}{to do good} ἢ κακοποιῆσαι,\FnParseFormGloss{d}{aorist active infinitive}{κακοποιέω}{to do evil} ψυχὴν σῶσαι\FnParse{e}{aorist active infinitive} ἢ ἀποκτεῖναι;\FnParse{f}{aorist active infinitive} οἱ δὲ ἐσιώπων.\FnParseFormGloss{g}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural}{σιωπάω}{to be quiet}

\MainTextVerseMark{4}{1}Καὶ πάλιν ἤρξατο\FnParse{a}{aorist middle indicative 3rd singular} διδάσκειν\FnParse{b}{present active infinitive} παρὰ τὴν θάλασσαν. καὶ ⸀συνάγεται\FnParse{c}{present passive indicative 3rd singular} πρὸς αὐτὸν ὄχλος ⸀πλεῖστος, ὥστε αὐτὸν ⸂εἰς πλοῖον ἐμβάντα⸃\FnParseFormGloss{d}{aorist active participle accusative masculine singular}{ἐμβαίνω}{to get into} καθῆσθαι\FnParse{e}{present middle infinitive} ἐν τῇ θαλάσσῃ, καὶ πᾶς ὁ ὄχλος πρὸς τὴν θάλασσαν ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς ⸀ἦσαν.\FnParse{f}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural}

\MainTextVerseMark{5}{1}Καὶ ἦλθον\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} εἰς τὸ πέραν\FnFormGloss{b}{πέραν}{on the other side} τῆς θαλάσσης εἰς τὴν χώραν\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative feminine singular}{χώρα}{country} τῶν ⸀Γερασηνῶν.\FnParseFormGloss{d}{genitive masculine plural}{Γερασηνός}{Gerasene}

\ChapterHeader{6}{Chapter 6}

\MainTextVerseMark{6}{1}Καὶ ἐξῆλθεν\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} ἐκεῖθεν,\FnFormGloss{b}{ἐκεῖθεν}{from there} καὶ ⸀ἔρχεται\FnParse{c}{present middle indicative 3rd singular} εἰς τὴν πατρίδα\FnParseFormGloss{d}{accusative feminine singular}{πατρίς}{hometown} αὐτοῦ, καὶ ἀκολουθοῦσιν\FnParse{e}{present active indicative 3rd plural} αὐτῷ οἱ μαθηταὶ αὐτοῦ.

\MainTextVerseMark{6}{3}οὐχ οὗτός ἐστιν\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 3rd singular} ὁ τέκτων,\FnParseFormGloss{b}{nominative masculine singular}{τέκτων}{carpenter} ὁ υἱὸς ⸀τῆς Μαρίας\FnParseFormGloss{c}{genitive feminine singular}{Μαρία}{Mary} ⸂καὶ ἀδελφὸς⸃ Ἰακώβου καὶ ⸀Ἰωσῆτος\FnParseFormGloss{d}{genitive masculine singular}{Ἰωσῆς}{Joses} καὶ Ἰούδα καὶ Σίμωνος; καὶ οὐκ εἰσὶν\FnParse{e}{present active indicative 3rd plural} αἱ ἀδελφαὶ\FnParseFormGloss{f}{nominative feminine plural}{ἀδελφή}{sister} αὐτοῦ ὧδε πρὸς ἡμᾶς; καὶ ἐσκανδαλίζοντο\FnParse{g}{imperfect passive indicative 3rd plural} ἐν αὐτῷ. 
\MainTextVerseMark{6}{4}⸂καὶ ἔλεγεν⸃\FnParse{a}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτοῖς ὁ Ἰησοῦς ὅτι Οὐκ ἔστιν\FnParse{b}{present active indicative 3rd singular} προφήτης ἄτιμος\FnParseFormGloss{c}{nominative masculine singular}{ἄτιμος}{without honor} εἰ μὴ ἐν τῇ πατρίδι\FnParseFormGloss{d}{dative feminine singular}{πατρίς}{hometown} αὐτοῦ καὶ ἐν τοῖς ⸂συγγενεῦσιν\FnParseFormGloss{e}{dative masculine plural}{συγγενής}{family} αὐτοῦ⸃ καὶ ἐν τῇ οἰκίᾳ αὐτοῦ.

Καὶ περιῆγεν\FnParseFormGloss{c}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular}{περιάγω}{to take} τὰς κώμας\FnParseFormGloss{d}{accusative feminine plural}{κώμη}{a village} κύκλῳ\FnFormGloss{e}{κύκλῳ}{all around} διδάσκων.\FnParse{f}{present active participle nominative masculine singular}

\ChapterHeader{10}{Chapter 10}

\MainTextVerseMark{10}{1}Καὶ ἐκεῖθεν\FnFormGloss{a}{ἐκεῖθεν}{from there} ἀναστὰς\FnParse{b}{aorist active participle nominative masculine singular} ἔρχεται\FnParse{c}{present middle indicative 3rd singular} εἰς τὰ ὅρια\FnParseFormGloss{d}{accusative neuter plural}{ὅριον}{region} τῆς Ἰουδαίας ⸀καὶ πέραν\FnFormGloss{e}{πέραν}{on the other side} τοῦ Ἰορδάνου,\FnParseFormGloss{f}{genitive masculine singular}{Ἰορδάνης}{Jordan} καὶ συμπορεύονται\FnParseFormGloss{g}{present middle indicative 3rd plural}{συμπορεύομαι}{to go with} πάλιν ὄχλοι πρὸς αὐτόν, καὶ ὡς εἰώθει\FnParseFormGloss{h}{pluperfect active indicative 3rd singular}{εἴωθα}{to have a custom} πάλιν ἐδίδασκεν\FnParse{i}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτούς.

\ChapterHeader{11}{Chapter 11}

\MainTextVerseMark{11}{1}Καὶ ὅτε ἐγγίζουσιν\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 3rd plural} εἰς Ἱεροσόλυμα εἰς Βηθφαγὴ\FnParseFormGloss{b}{accusative feminine singular}{Βηθφαγή}{Bethphage} καὶ Βηθανίαν\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative feminine singular}{Βηθανία}{Bethany} πρὸς τὸ Ὄρος τῶν Ἐλαιῶν,\FnParseFormGloss{d}{genitive feminine plural}{ἐλαία}{olive} ἀποστέλλει\FnParse{e}{present active indicative 3rd singular} δύο τῶν μαθητῶν αὐτοῦ 
\MainTextVerseMark{11}{2}καὶ λέγει\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτοῖς· Ὑπάγετε\FnParse{b}{present active imperative 2nd plural} εἰς τὴν κώμην\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative feminine singular}{κώμη}{a village} τὴν κατέναντι\FnFormGloss{d}{κατέναντι}{ahead} ὑμῶν, καὶ ⸀εὐθὺς εἰσπορευόμενοι\FnParseFormGloss{e}{present middle participle nominative masculine plural}{εἰσπορεύομαι}{to go in} εἰς αὐτὴν εὑρήσετε\FnParse{f}{future active indicative 2nd plural} πῶλον\FnParseFormGloss{g}{accusative masculine singular}{πῶλος}{colt} δεδεμένον\FnParse{h}{perfect passive participle accusative masculine singular} ἐφ’ ὃν οὐδεὶς ⸀οὔπω\FnFormGloss{i}{οὔπω}{not yet} ἀνθρώπων ⸀ἐκάθισεν·\FnParse{j}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} ⸂λύσατε\FnParse{k}{aorist active imperative 2nd plural} αὐτὸν καὶ φέρετε⸃.\FnParse{l}{present active imperative 2nd plural} 
\MainTextVerseMark{11}{3}καὶ ἐάν τις ὑμῖν εἴπῃ·\FnParse{a}{aorist active subjunctive 3rd singular} Τί ποιεῖτε\FnParse{b}{present active indicative 2nd plural} τοῦτο; εἴπατε\FnParse{c}{aorist active imperative 2nd plural} ⸀ὅτι Ὁ κύριος αὐτοῦ χρείαν ἔχει·\FnParse{d}{present active indicative 3rd singular} καὶ ⸀εὐθὺς αὐτὸν ἀποστέλλει\FnParse{e}{present active indicative 3rd singular} ⸀πάλιν ὧδε. 
\MainTextVerseMark{11}{4}⸂καὶ ἀπῆλθον⸃\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} καὶ εὗρον\FnParse{b}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} πῶλον\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative masculine singular}{πῶλος}{colt} δεδεμένον\FnParse{d}{perfect passive participle accusative masculine singular} ⸀πρὸς θύραν ἔξω ἐπὶ τοῦ ἀμφόδου,\FnParseFormGloss{e}{genitive neuter singular}{ἄμφοδον}{street} καὶ λύουσιν\FnParse{f}{present active indicative 3rd plural} αὐτόν.

\MainTextVerseMark{11}{6}οἱ δὲ εἶπαν\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} αὐτοῖς καθὼς ⸀εἶπεν\FnParse{b}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} ὁ Ἰησοῦς· καὶ ἀφῆκαν\FnParse{c}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} αὐτούς.

\MainTextVerseMark{13}{1}Καὶ ἐκπορευομένου\FnParse{a}{present middle participle genitive masculine singular} αὐτοῦ ἐκ τοῦ ἱεροῦ λέγει\FnParse{b}{present active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτῷ εἷς τῶν μαθητῶν αὐτοῦ· Διδάσκαλε, ἴδε ποταποὶ\FnParseFormGloss{c}{nominative masculine plural}{ποταπός}{of what kind?} λίθοι καὶ ποταπαὶ\FnParseFormGloss{d}{nominative feminine plural}{ποταπός}{of what kind?} οἰκοδομαί.\FnParseFormGloss{e}{nominative feminine plural}{οἰκοδομή}{building} 
\MainTextVerseMark{13}{2}καὶ ὁ ⸀Ἰησοῦς εἶπεν\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτῷ· Βλέπεις\FnParse{b}{present active indicative 2nd singular} ταύτας τὰς μεγάλας οἰκοδομάς;\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative feminine plural}{οἰκοδομή}{building} οὐ μὴ ἀφεθῇ\FnParse{d}{aorist passive subjunctive 3rd singular} ⸀ὧδε λίθος ἐπὶ ⸀λίθον ὃς οὐ μὴ καταλυθῇ.\FnParseFormGloss{e}{aorist passive subjunctive 3rd singular}{καταλύω}{throw down} 
\MainTextVerseMark{13}{3}Καὶ καθημένου\FnParse{a}{present middle participle genitive masculine singular} αὐτοῦ εἰς τὸ Ὄρος τῶν Ἐλαιῶν\FnParseFormGloss{b}{genitive feminine plural}{ἐλαία}{olive} κατέναντι\FnFormGloss{c}{κατέναντι}{ahead} τοῦ ἱεροῦ ⸀ἐπηρώτα\FnParse{d}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular} αὐτὸν κατ’ ἰδίαν Πέτρος καὶ Ἰάκωβος καὶ Ἰωάννης καὶ Ἀνδρέας·\FnParseFormGloss{e}{nominative masculine singular}{Ἀνδρέας}{Andrew} 
\MainTextVerseMark{13}{4}Εἰπὸν\FnParse{a}{aorist active imperative 2nd singular} ἡμῖν πότε\FnFormGloss{b}{πότε}{when? how long?} ταῦτα ἔσται,\FnParse{c}{future middle indicative 3rd singular} καὶ τί τὸ σημεῖον ὅταν μέλλῃ\FnParse{d}{present active subjunctive 3rd singular} ⸂ταῦτα συντελεῖσθαι\FnParseFormGloss{e}{present passive infinitive}{συντελέω}{to finish} πάντα⸃.

\MainTextVerseMark{13}{7}ὅταν δὲ ⸀ἀκούσητε\FnParse{a}{aorist active subjunctive 2nd plural} πολέμους\FnParseFormGloss{b}{accusative masculine plural}{πόλεμος}{war} καὶ ἀκοὰς\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative feminine plural}{ἀκοή}{hearing} πολέμων,\FnParseFormGloss{d}{genitive masculine plural}{πόλεμος}{war} μὴ θροεῖσθε·\FnParseFormGloss{e}{present passive imperative 2nd plural}{θροέομαι}{to be alarmed} ⸀δεῖ\FnParse{f}{present active indicative 3rd singular} γενέσθαι,\FnParse{g}{aorist middle infinitive} ἀλλ’ οὔπω\FnFormGloss{h}{οὔπω}{not yet} τὸ τέλος.

\ChapterHeader{14}{Chapter 14}

\MainTextVerseMark{14}{1}Ἦν\FnParse{a}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular} δὲ τὸ πάσχα\FnParseFormGloss{b}{nominative neuter singular}{πάσχα}{Passover} καὶ τὰ ἄζυμα\FnParseFormGloss{c}{nominative neuter plural}{ἄζυμος}{unleavened} μετὰ δύο ἡμέρας. καὶ ἐζήτουν\FnParse{d}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural} οἱ ἀρχιερεῖς καὶ οἱ γραμματεῖς πῶς αὐτὸν ἐν δόλῳ\FnParseFormGloss{e}{dative masculine singular}{δόλος}{deceit} κρατήσαντες\FnParse{f}{aorist active participle nominative masculine plural} ἀποκτείνωσιν,\FnParse{g}{aorist active subjunctive 3rd plural} 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{2}ἔλεγον\FnParse{a}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural} ⸀γάρ· Μὴ ἐν τῇ ἑορτῇ,\FnParseFormGloss{b}{dative feminine singular}{ἑορτή}{feast} μήποτε\FnFormGloss{c}{μήποτε}{never} ⸂ἔσται\FnParse{d}{future middle indicative 3rd singular} θόρυβος⸃\FnParseFormGloss{e}{nominative masculine singular}{θόρυβος}{uproar} τοῦ λαοῦ. 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{3}Καὶ ὄντος\FnParse{a}{present active participle genitive masculine singular} αὐτοῦ ἐν Βηθανίᾳ\FnParseFormGloss{b}{dative feminine singular}{Βηθανία}{Bethany} ἐν τῇ οἰκίᾳ Σίμωνος τοῦ λεπροῦ\FnParseFormGloss{c}{genitive masculine singular}{λεπρός}{leprous} κατακειμένου\FnParseFormGloss{d}{present middle participle genitive masculine singular}{κατάκειμαι}{to lie down} αὐτοῦ ἦλθεν\FnParse{e}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} γυνὴ ἔχουσα\FnParse{f}{present active participle nominative feminine singular} ἀλάβαστρον\FnParseFormGloss{g}{accusative feminine singular}{ἀλάβαστρος}{alabaster jar} μύρου\FnParseFormGloss{h}{genitive neuter singular}{μύρον}{perfume} νάρδου\FnParseFormGloss{i}{genitive feminine singular}{νάρδος}{nard} πιστικῆς\FnParseFormGloss{j}{genitive feminine singular}{πιστικός}{pure} πολυτελοῦς·\FnParseFormGloss{k}{genitive feminine singular}{πολυτελής}{expensive} ⸀συντρίψασα\FnParseFormGloss{l}{aorist active participle nominative feminine singular}{συντρίβω}{to break} ⸀τὴν ἀλάβαστρον\FnParseFormGloss{m}{accusative feminine singular}{ἀλάβαστρος}{alabaster jar} κατέχεεν\FnParseFormGloss{n}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular}{καταχέω}{to pour out} ⸀αὐτοῦ τῆς κεφαλῆς. 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{4}ἦσαν\FnParse{a}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural} δέ τινες ἀγανακτοῦντες\FnParseFormGloss{b}{present active participle nominative masculine plural}{ἀγανακτέω}{to be indignant} πρὸς ⸀ἑαυτούς· Εἰς τί ἡ ἀπώλεια\FnParseFormGloss{c}{nominative feminine singular}{ἀπώλεια}{destruction} αὕτη τοῦ μύρου\FnParseFormGloss{d}{genitive neuter singular}{μύρον}{perfume} γέγονεν;\FnParse{e}{perfect active indicative 3rd singular} 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{5}ἠδύνατο\FnParse{a}{imperfect middle indicative 3rd singular} γὰρ τοῦτο ⸂τὸ μύρον⸃\FnParseFormGloss{b}{nominative neuter singular}{μύρον}{perfume} πραθῆναι\FnParseFormGloss{c}{aorist passive infinitive}{πιπράσκω}{to sell} ἐπάνω\FnFormGloss{d}{ἐπάνω}{above} ⸂δηναρίων\FnParseFormGloss{e}{genitive neuter plural}{δηνάριον}{denarius} τριακοσίων⸃\FnParseFormGloss{f}{genitive neuter plural}{τριακόσιοι}{three hundred} καὶ δοθῆναι\FnParse{g}{aorist passive infinitive} τοῖς πτωχοῖς· καὶ ἐνεβριμῶντο\FnParseFormGloss{h}{imperfect middle indicative 3rd plural}{ἐμβριμάομαι}{to warn sternly} αὐτῇ. 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{6}ὁ δὲ Ἰησοῦς εἶπεν·\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} Ἄφετε\FnParse{b}{aorist active imperative 2nd plural} αὐτήν· τί αὐτῇ κόπους\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative masculine plural}{κόπος}{labor} παρέχετε;\FnParseFormGloss{d}{present active indicative 2nd plural}{παρέχω}{to present} καλὸν ἔργον ἠργάσατο\FnParse{e}{aorist middle indicative 3rd singular} ἐν ἐμοί· 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{7}πάντοτε γὰρ τοὺς πτωχοὺς ἔχετε\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 2nd plural} μεθ’ ἑαυτῶν, καὶ ὅταν θέλητε\FnParse{b}{present active subjunctive 2nd plural} δύνασθε\FnParse{c}{present middle indicative 2nd plural} ⸀αὐτοῖς εὖ\FnFormGloss{d}{εὖ}{well} ποιῆσαι,\FnParse{e}{aorist active infinitive} ἐμὲ δὲ οὐ πάντοτε ἔχετε·\FnParse{f}{present active indicative 2nd plural} 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{8}ὃ ⸀ἔσχεν\FnParse{a}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} ἐποίησεν,\FnParse{b}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} προέλαβεν\FnParseFormGloss{c}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular}{προλαμβάνω}{to take beforehand} μυρίσαι\FnParseFormGloss{d}{aorist active infinitive}{μυρίζω}{to pour perfume} ⸂τὸ σῶμά μου⸃ εἰς τὸν ἐνταφιασμόν.\FnParseFormGloss{e}{accusative masculine singular}{ἐνταφιασμός}{preparation for burial} 
\MainTextVerseMark{14}{9}ἀμὴν ⸀δὲ λέγω\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 1st singular} ὑμῖν, ὅπου ⸀ἐὰν κηρυχθῇ\FnParse{b}{aorist passive subjunctive 3rd singular} τὸ ⸀εὐαγγέλιον εἰς ὅλον τὸν κόσμον, καὶ ὃ ἐποίησεν\FnParse{c}{aorist active indicative 3rd singular} αὕτη λαληθήσεται\FnParse{d}{future passive indicative 3rd singular} εἰς μνημόσυνον\FnParseFormGloss{e}{accusative neuter singular}{μνημόσυνον}{memory} αὐτῆς.

\ChapterHeader{15}{Chapter 15}

\MainTextVerseMark{15}{1}Καὶ ⸀εὐθὺς πρωῒ\FnFormGloss{a}{πρωΐ}{early in the morning} συμβούλιον\FnParseFormGloss{b}{accusative neuter singular}{συμβούλιον}{plan} ποιήσαντες\FnParse{c}{aorist active participle nominative masculine plural} οἱ ἀρχιερεῖς μετὰ τῶν πρεσβυτέρων καὶ γραμματέων καὶ ὅλον τὸ συνέδριον\FnParseFormGloss{d}{nominative neuter singular}{συνέδριον}{Sanhedrin} δήσαντες\FnParse{e}{aorist active participle nominative masculine plural} τὸν Ἰησοῦν ἀπήνεγκαν\FnParseFormGloss{f}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural}{ἀποφέρω}{to carry away} καὶ ⸀παρέδωκαν\FnParse{g}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} Πιλάτῳ.

\MainTextVerseMark{15}{16}Οἱ δὲ στρατιῶται\FnParseFormGloss{a}{nominative masculine plural}{στρατιώτης}{soldier} ἀπήγαγον\FnParseFormGloss{b}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural}{ἀπάγω}{to lead away} αὐτὸν ἔσω\FnFormGloss{c}{ἔσω}{in} τῆς αὐλῆς,\FnParseFormGloss{d}{genitive feminine singular}{αὐλή}{palace} ὅ ἐστιν\FnParse{e}{present active indicative 3rd singular} πραιτώριον,\FnParseFormGloss{f}{nominative neuter singular}{πραιτώριον}{Praetorium} καὶ συγκαλοῦσιν\FnParseFormGloss{g}{present active indicative 3rd plural}{συγκαλέω}{to call together} ὅλην τὴν σπεῖραν.\FnParseFormGloss{h}{accusative feminine singular}{σπεῖρα}{company of soldiers}

\ChapterHeader{16}{Chapter 16}

\MainTextVerseMark{16}{1}Καὶ διαγενομένου\FnParseFormGloss{a}{aorist middle participle genitive neuter singular}{διαγίνομαι}{to pass} τοῦ σαββάτου ⸀Μαρία\FnParseFormGloss{b}{nominative feminine singular}{Μαρία}{Mary} ἡ Μαγδαληνὴ\FnParseFormGloss{c}{nominative feminine singular}{Μαγδαληνή}{Magdalene} καὶ Μαρία\FnParseFormGloss{d}{nominative feminine singular}{Μαρία}{Mary} ⸂ἡ τοῦ⸃ Ἰακώβου καὶ Σαλώμη\FnParseFormGloss{e}{nominative feminine singular}{Σαλώμη}{Salome} ἠγόρασαν\FnParse{f}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} ἀρώματα\FnParseFormGloss{g}{accusative neuter plural}{ἄρωμα}{spices} ἵνα ἐλθοῦσαι\FnParse{h}{aorist active participle nominative feminine plural} ἀλείψωσιν\FnParseFormGloss{i}{aorist active subjunctive 3rd plural}{ἀλείφω}{to pour on} αὐτόν. 
\MainTextVerseMark{16}{2}καὶ λίαν\FnFormGloss{a}{λίαν}{very much} πρωῒ\FnFormGloss{b}{πρωΐ}{early in the morning} ⸂τῇ μιᾷ τῶν⸃ σαββάτων ἔρχονται\FnParse{c}{present middle indicative 3rd plural} ἐπὶ τὸ μνημεῖον ἀνατείλαντος\FnParseFormGloss{d}{aorist active participle genitive masculine singular}{ἀνατέλλω}{to rise} τοῦ ἡλίου. 
\MainTextVerseMark{16}{3}καὶ ἔλεγον\FnParse{a}{imperfect active indicative 3rd plural} πρὸς ἑαυτάς· Τίς ἀποκυλίσει\FnParseFormGloss{b}{future active indicative 3rd singular}{ἀποκυλίω}{to roll away} ἡμῖν τὸν λίθον ⸀ἐκ τῆς θύρας τοῦ μνημείου; 
\MainTextVerseMark{16}{4}καὶ ἀναβλέψασαι\FnParseFormGloss{a}{aorist active participle nominative feminine plural}{ἀναβλέπω}{to look up} θεωροῦσιν\FnParse{b}{present active indicative 3rd plural} ὅτι ⸀ἀποκεκύλισται\FnParseFormGloss{c}{perfect passive indicative 3rd singular}{ἀποκυλίω}{to roll away} ὁ λίθος, ἦν\FnParse{d}{imperfect active indicative 3rd singular} γὰρ μέγας σφόδρα.\FnFormGloss{e}{σφόδρα}{very} 
\MainTextVerseMark{16}{5}καὶ εἰσελθοῦσαι\FnParse{a}{aorist active participle nominative feminine plural} εἰς τὸ μνημεῖον εἶδον\FnParse{b}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} νεανίσκον\FnParseFormGloss{c}{accusative masculine singular}{νεανίσκος}{young man} καθήμενον\FnParse{d}{present middle participle accusative masculine singular} ἐν τοῖς δεξιοῖς περιβεβλημένον\FnParseFormGloss{e}{perfect middle participle accusative masculine singular}{περιβάλλω}{to dress} στολὴν\FnParseFormGloss{f}{accusative feminine singular}{στολή}{robe} λευκήν,\FnParseFormGloss{g}{accusative feminine singular}{λευκός}{white} καὶ ἐξεθαμβήθησαν.\FnParseFormGloss{h}{aorist passive indicative 3rd plural}{ἐκθαμβέομαι}{to be overwhelmed with wonder} 
\MainTextVerseMark{16}{6}ὁ δὲ λέγει\FnParse{a}{present active indicative 3rd singular} αὐταῖς· Μὴ ἐκθαμβεῖσθε·\FnParseFormGloss{b}{present passive imperative 2nd plural}{ἐκθαμβέομαι}{to be overwhelmed with wonder} Ἰησοῦν ζητεῖτε\FnParse{c}{present active indicative 2nd plural} τὸν Ναζαρηνὸν\FnParseFormGloss{d}{accusative masculine singular}{Ναζαρηνός}{of Nazareth} τὸν ἐσταυρωμένον·\FnParse{e}{perfect passive participle accusative masculine singular} ἠγέρθη,\FnParse{f}{aorist passive indicative 3rd singular} οὐκ ἔστιν\FnParse{g}{present active indicative 3rd singular} ὧδε· ἴδε ὁ τόπος ὅπου ἔθηκαν\FnParse{h}{aorist active indicative 3rd plural} αὐτόν·
